border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">旺盛的市场需求<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">催生了制售酒品及其相关行业的兴起，</span>类似于蒂华纳的边境小城凭借其区位优势吸引了买卖双方，借此强势崛起，先是有了第一条马路——革命大街，便利游客交通的同时美化了市容；之后又建立了酒吧、旅店，满足边境客人的餐饮需求。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">革命大街是蒂华纳第一条建造的道路</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">酒吧，酒店，妓院等也多集中在这里</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">现是蒂华纳的市中心</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Denis Kabanov / Shutterstock）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKWAuX3JlLWcCe7Wr7CgJcTsaVACuZmK7G5dETgQtytdB9pLJ6vBR8Y6ichZzghm93gxMcRtNjAwZDw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">随着招待美国游客的场所越来越多，它们也逐渐出现了满足不同消费水平客人的分化。像阿瓜卡莲特（Agua Caliente）<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">这样的住宿、水疗、赌博、高尔夫球等休闲运动一条龙服务的度假综合体</span>深受有钱人欢迎，好莱坞明星出入其间的花边新闻则进一步抬高了这一地区的知名度，让美国游客趋之若鹜。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">南加州的富人们来到这个不被管制的新兴娱乐胜地</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">在美国本土被禁止的赛马，饮酒，性交易等</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">在这里随处可得</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（1928年的阿瓜卡莲特酒店）</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：San Diego History Center Photo Archive.）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"901\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKWAuX3JlLWcCe7Wr7CgJcTsAxdgZayQTrUmDAEicweWTtebpWhRib2icgHnME9TIq7Hib4GuqibEXSAoRQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">在当时的蒂华纳，赌博是合法的，娼妓行业则处在屡禁不止的灰色地带。而正因为美国大多数地区禁止这些行业，美国人只能来到蒂华纳解决这些需求，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">蒂华纳的灰色产业名气因此越来越大，</span>游客来蒂华纳的目的也来越来明确，最终形成了一种畸形的产业繁荣。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">豪车，美女，香槟，泳池...</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">全方面满足顾客需求</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：</span>Official Hong Kong Gentlemen's Club/YouTube<span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">）</span></span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 90%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.7112069\" data-type=\"gif\" data-w=\"464\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/DCftNYRGoKWAuX3JlLWcCe7Wr7CgJcTsfdGPzpNrzTZybYLkk1jB7XQAetyjs4GY6YaKQ4oDFB76IuicvVibEkQQ/640?wx_fmt=gif\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">经过30年代墨西哥政府出手打击赌博业，蒂华纳的赌博业一度衰落，但是毕竟这里距离墨西哥首都遥远，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">而墨西哥政策走向常因不同派别上台变更，</span>所以赌博业并未消失。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">60年代时，墨西哥政府借助<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">地价和人力成本低的优势</span>在边境城市发展工业，提升了蒂华纳城产业的丰富程度，也吸引了大量墨西哥人搬到这里。之后，甚至从中南美洲偷渡美国的人也会选择此地作为中转站，或索性留在机会比老家更多的蒂华纳。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">大量人口在此流动，宽松的管控</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">也就会产生更多的谋生机会</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Sherry V Smith / Shutterstock.com）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKWAuX3JlLWcCe7Wr7CgJcTsIoXm0NLozwoq4qDsibdh8Csm33OW5l79BBIqLWwxF9PxHdDiakC7WxLw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">大量涌入的男性劳动力导致城市的性别比例失衡，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">潜在需求让色情业迅速下沉，</span>非法的暗娼大量出现。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">灰色产业看似成为了法外之地，实则内部有一套更为严酷的竞争规则，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">想要形成规模势必需要黑恶势力站台。</span>而黑恶势力关注的不是发展行业本身，而是行业带来的暴利。随着70年代哥伦比亚毒品扩散全美洲，毒品卡特尔在墨西哥出现，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">他们成为了蒂华纳的无冕之王，</span>帮派火拼、抢劫、贩毒、贩卖人口等恶行暴力事件层出不穷。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">各地区的贩毒家族组织之间的竞争</span><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">以及和政府的对抗</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">带来了大量的枪战，杀戮事件</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：https://www.eluniversal.com.mx）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(226, 224, 224);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.8574074074074074\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKWAuX3JlLWcCe7Wr7CgJcTseoibYpysYo6HnGOiaVpaKVxiawZuczY54S4uRUAjbImJnIuBMYlP9m1Ig/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">但是，不仅美国人民南下消费的热情没有因为这些安全问题消退，游客源甚至<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">扩大到了万里之外的日本、中国。</span></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;color: rgb(189, 112, 112);font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"> </p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">疫情冲击色情业</p></section><section style=\"margin: 8px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(189, 112, 112);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">随着<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">北美自贸协定</span>的签订，美国与墨西哥的经济联系日趋紧密，墨西<span style=\"color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\">哥人可以相对容易地获得赴美工作签证，不少人也拿到了</span><span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">美墨双重国籍。</span>处于家庭成员分布两地的原因，这些人也往往在两国之间来回奔波。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这样的盛况其实是常态了</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">过境和过一个收费站一样方便</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Chad Zuber / Shutterstock.com）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKWAuX3JlLWcCe7Wr7CgJcTsNvyeiaZdICIRK0rj5HKP18hesr2EeNP3hW7oFIzEF7icOCbIOKgsTelQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">随着2月27日墨西哥出现第一例确诊，虽然墨西哥政府对内要求隔离，对外要求减少美墨边境不必要的过境，但是拦不住这些有<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">双重身份的墨西哥人。</span>到五月末，每天依旧有数千辆车穿梭在美国墨西哥之间，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">定义模糊的政策根本无法阻止新冠的传播，</span>几个月的时间中确诊人数逐步攀升，累计确诊早已超过50万人，排名全球第六。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">死亡率也名列前茅</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Omar Franco Perez / Shutterstock.com）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKWAuX3JlLWcCe7Wr7CgJcTsJQ10aXicSB5JedEsYKNbPKpn1qAslibib6THPcrryOxqgkMZLHmDrZ61A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">蒂华纳这样的边境大城连接着美国最重要、墨西哥裔占比最高的加州，每日过境人数可想而知。不巧的是加州此时已然成为美国疫情的重灾区，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">所以蒂华纳被传播的风险极大，</span>几乎必然是墨西哥的疫情小中心。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">但反常的是，目前墨西哥疫情的重灾区<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">是人口密度惊人的墨西哥城，</span>蒂华纳的确诊人数与其作为边境口岸的重要性并不相称。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">墨西哥城向合法的性工作者发放了经济补助</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">也是怕她们迫于生计偷偷营业</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Eduardo Mejia / Shutterstock.com）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">但死亡率</span>揭示了其中的猫腻。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">在3.5%以下，</span>在经济条件相对较差，政府承认确诊数被低估的伊朗，死亡率也仅有5.7%，墨西哥的死亡率却高达10.9%。更诡异的是蒂华纳所在的南加州，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">确诊病例死亡率高达到19.3%，</span>令人瞠目结舌，因此该地确诊病例数字实在可疑。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">在政府注册的合法性工作者，</span>在蒂华纳，她们在被称为Zona Norte的红灯区内工作，定期接受身体检查。合法的声色场所要满足定位标准、清洁标准、营业时间等政府规定，也免不了需要交税。另一类则是<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">屡禁不止的暗娼，</span>近年来与时俱进，利用社交媒体也做起了互联网+，查处难度变得更大。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">他们注射毒品的概率是其他男性的四倍，</span>当然也就更可能传播种种疾病。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Chad Zuber / Shutterstock）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(226, 224, 224);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKWAuX3JlLWcCe7Wr7CgJcTsMC7qoBOkSVicia1gITIfEib6ibVia42JBgRJeoVMW2kFaPkcx9aayn6eGSw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">到8月初，相关行业终于无法蒙受损失，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">超过80家夜总会向州政府请愿要求重新开放，</span>一千余名相关从业人员走上街头向政府施压。</p></section><section style=\"margin-top: 6px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">情色行业同时也拉动了墨西哥旅游业</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">政府的压力也很大</span></p><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：hongkonggc/ ins）</span>▼<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1161\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKWAuX3JlLWcCe7Wr7CgJcTsOu5LefP8EXaL7Oib3KW2Kulh5KCDdVavObhvibqicmZtoy2wc1DZCTlsA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">8月10日，疫情中心墨西哥城酒吧作为餐厅重新开放，营业时间截至晚上十点，允许顾客达到满员量的30%。不知道这一政策松动会不会<span style=\"color: rgb(58, 58, 58);box-sizing: border-box;\">引起南加州政府的效仿。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p></section><section style=\"margin: 8px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(189, 112, 112);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">继续封锁依旧无法阻止少数人关门营业，也无法短期内阻止新冠肆虐。<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">部分放开又必然会导致疫情的进一步失控，</span>甚至出现向上的拐点。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\">这是蒂华纳结构问题发展至今被新冠暴露出的尴尬，也是墨西哥整体的一个缩影。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"font-size: 10px;color: rgba(74, 72, 72, 0.5);line-height: 1.9;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing:
